+ \"'\"\n\t\t\t\t\t+ \"  Expected method name: \" + opImplName;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn opImpl.call(this, ctx, ast);\n\t\t\tcase \"FunctionCall\":\n\t\t\t\tlet fnImplName = \"fn_\" + \"'\"\n\t\t\t\t\t+ \"  Expected method name: \" + fnImplName;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\treturn fnImpl.call(this, ctx, ast);\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\tthrow \"Unsupported language construct '\" + ast.type + \"'.\"\n\t\t\t\t+ \"  AST: \" + JSON.stringify(ast);\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\n\t// NODE & PATH\n\n\tNodeSet(ctx, ast, forceRelative) {\n\n\t\tlet nodes = ast.nodes.slice(0);\n\n\t\t// If the first AST is a /descendant-or-self::node()/\"\t\n\t\t\t\t// - see https://www.w3.org/TR/1999/REC-xpath-19991116/#path-abbrev\n\n\t\t\t\tlet canUseTagNameTuple = this.useTagNameInDescendantSearch(ctx, nodes, or else the children are presented in the wrong order\n\t\t\t\t// - see failing tests when the next line is commented out\n\t\t\t\t// - not sure why\n\t\t\t\tsortNext = true;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse if recurse(args, depth, resolvedArgs, functionImpl) {\n\n\t\t\tif (depth >= args.length) {\n\t\t\t\t// Only happens for no-arg functions.\n\t\t\t\treturn functionImpl([]);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t// Support for {\n\n\tctx.nodeSet.sort(function (e1, e2) {\n\n\t\tif (!e1.compareDocumentPosition && isAttr(e1)) {\n\t\t\te1 = e1.ownerElement;\n\t\t}\n\t\tif (!e2.compareDocumentPosition && isAttr(e2)) {\n\t\t\te2 !node.parentNode) && node.host;\n}\n\nfunction getDocument(node) {\n\twhile (true) {\n\t\tif (node.nodeName === nodeNames.DOCUMENT || (node.nodeName === nodeNames.HTML && !node.parentNode)) {\n\t\t\treturn node;\n\t\t}\n\t\tnode = isShadowRoot(node) ? node.host : node.parentNode;\n\t}\n}\n\nfunction isSlotWithSuppliedContent(node) {\n\n\tif (!isElement(node) || node.localName !== nodeNames.SLOT) {\n\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\n\t// Find the hosting element\n\tlet shadowRoot = node.parentNode;\n\twhile (shadowRoot && !shadowRoot.host) {\n\t\tshadowRoot = shadowRoot.parentNode;\n\t}\n\tif (!shadowRoot) {\n\t\treturn false;\n\t}\n\tlet host = shadowRoot.host;\n\n\t// Get the slot name, if any.\n\tlet slotName = node.getAttribute('name');\n\n\tlet hostChild = host.firstChild;\n\twhile (hostChild) {\n\t\tif (isElement(hostChild)) {\n\t\t\tif (hostChild.getAttribute('slot') === slotName) {\n\t\t\t\treturn true;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (!slotName) {\n\t\t\t// Text nodes count as content for the unnamed slot.\n\t\t\treturn true;\n\t\t}\n\t\thostChild = hostChild.nextSibling;\n\t}\n\treturn false;\n}\n\nfunction nextSiblingForSuppliedContent(node) {\n\tconst host = node.parentNode;\n\tlet childIndex = -1;\n\tfor (let i = 0; i \u003C host.childElementCount; i++) {\n\t\tif (host.children[i] == node) null;\n}\n\nfunction slotHasAssignedNodes(node) {\n\tconst assignedNodes = node.assignedNodes();\n\treturn assignedNodes && assignedNodes.length > 0;\n}\n\nfunction getSlotTextContent(node) {\n\tif (slotHasAssignedNodes(node)) {\n\t\tconst textContent = node.assignedNodes().reduce((t, e) => t += e.nodeType === Node.TEXT_NODE ? e.textContent : '', '');\n\t\tif (textContent) {\n\t\t\treturn textContent;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn node.textContent;\n}\n\nfunction getParentNode(currentNode) {\n\tif (!currentNode) {\n\t\treturn;\n\t}\n\n\tif (currentNode.assignedSlot) {\n\t\treturn currentNode.assignedSlot;\n\t} else if (currentNode.nodeName === nodeNames.DOCUMENT_FRAGMENT) {\n\t\treturn currentNode.host;\n\t} else {\n\t\treturn currentNode.parentNode;\n\t}\n}\n\nfunction getNextSibling(currentNode) {\n\tif (!currentNode) {\n\t\treturn;\n\t}\n\n\tif ((currentNode.nodeName === nodeNames.DOCUMENT_FRAGMENT)) {\n\t\tconst childNodes = nextSibling.nextSibling;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunction getNextSiblingInsideSlot(currentNode) {\n\tconst slotElem = currentNode.assignedSlot;\n\tconst children = slotElem.assignedNodes();\n\tconst indexOfCurrentNode = children.indexOf(currentNode);\n\tif (children.length - 1 === indexOfCurrentNode) {\n\t\treturn null;\n\t} else {\n\t\treturn children[indexOfCurrentNode + 1];\n\t}\n}\n\nfunction hasSameOrNoSlot(currentNode) {\n\tconst nextSibling = currentNode.nextSibling || {};\n\tconst haveNoSlot = !currentNode.assignedSlot && !nextSibling.assignedSlot;\n\tconst haveSameSlot = currentNode.assignedSlot === nextSibling.assignedSlot;\n\treturn haveNoSlot || haveSameSlot;\n}\n\nfunction listParentNodes(node) {\n\tlet parentNodes = [];\n\twhile (node) {\n\t\tif (node.nodeName === '#document-fragment') {\n\t\t\tnode = node.host;\n\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t}\n\t\tif (node.assignedSlot) {\n\t\t\tnode = if(el) {
	if (isIEDriver) {
		// In case of IE-Browser by scrollIntoView() we moving towards the element but it will move to the top view of that 
		// element. To align the element to center we do calculation on Pixels of the current screen.  
		el.scrollIntoView();
		var top = el.getBoundingClientRect().top;
		var middleY = window.innerHeight/2;
		var offsetY = 0;
		if (top < middleY) {
		 offsetY = middleY - top;
		}
		window.scroll(0,window.pageYOffset-offsetY);
	} else {
		if (el.tagName === 'SLOT') {
			el = el.parentNode ? el.parentNode : el;
		}
		if (el.closest('div.listViewContent.slds-table--header-fixed_container')) {
			if (isFirefoxDriver) {
				el.scrollIntoView({ block: "nearest" });	
			} else {
				el.scrollIntoViewIfNeeded({ behaviour: "smooth" });	
			}
		} else {
			el.scrollIntoView({ block: "center", behaviour: "smooth" });
		}
	}
}
